<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top: 12pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff;">PART
I</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top: 12pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff;">Item 1. Business</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 20pt; background-color: #ffffff">N/A</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top: 12pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff;">Item 1A. Risk
Factors</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 20pt; background-color: #ffffff">N/A</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top: 12pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff;">Item 1B. Unresolved Staff
Comments</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 20pt; background-color: #ffffff">N/A</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top: 12pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff;">Item 2. Properties</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 20pt; background-color: #ffffff">The Honda Auto
Receivables 2004-1 Owner Trust (the
&lsquo;&lsquo;Trust&rsquo;&rsquo;) is a statutory trust formed
pursuant to the trust agreement (the
&lsquo;&lsquo;Agreement&rsquo;&rsquo;) between American Honda
Receivables Corp., as Depositor (the
&lsquo;&lsquo;Depositor&rsquo;&rsquo;), and U.S. Bank Trust
National Association, as Owner Trustee.</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Trust
has issued four classes of notes (&lsquo;&lsquo;Class A-1 Notes
1.13875%&rsquo;&rsquo;; &lsquo;&lsquo;Class A-2 Notes
1.68%&rsquo;&rsquo;; &lsquo;&lsquo;Class A-3 Notes
2.40%&rsquo;&rsquo; and &lsquo;&lsquo;Class A-4 Notes
3.06%&rsquo;&rsquo;; collectively, the
&lsquo;&lsquo;Notes&rsquo;&rsquo;) and a class of certificates (the
&lsquo;&lsquo;Certificates&rsquo;&rsquo;). The Notes are backed by
a pledge of the Trust&rsquo;s assets. Interest and principal
collections from the Trust&rsquo;s assets will be divided among the
various classes of securities in specified proportions. The
Trust&rsquo;s assets include fixed rate motor vehicles retail
installment sales contracts secured by new and used Honda and Acura
motor vehicles (the
&lsquo;&lsquo;Receivables&rsquo;&rsquo;).</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 20pt; background-color: #ffffff">The following
tables set forth the number and aggregate principal amount of
delinquent receivables, the delinquency rates, and aggregate net losses
of the Honda Auto Receivables 2004-1 Owner Trust as of March
31,  2006:</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 6pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff">1. Delinquent

Proceedings</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 20pt; background-color: #ffffff">N/A</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top: 12pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff;">Item 4. Submission of Matters to a Vote
of Security Holders</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 6pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 20pt; background-color: #ffffff">No vote or consent of the holders of the
Notes (the &lsquo;&lsquo;Noteholders&rsquo;&rsquo;) was solicited
for any purpose during the year ended March  31,
2006.</p>

<hr width="760" style="padding-left: 0pt;" align="left">
<br>
<page>
<a name="page"></a>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top: 12pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff;">PART II</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff">
<font style="font-weight: bold; font-style: normal;">Item 5. Market
For Registrant&rsquo;s Common Equity, Related Stockholder Matters and
Issuer Purchases of Equity Securities</font>
</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 20pt; background-color: #ffffff">All Certificates issued
by Honda Auto Receivables 2004-1 Owner Trust are held by American Honda
Receivables Corp. All holders of record of the Notes issued by Honda
Auto Receivables 2004-1 Owner Trust are registered through Cede &amp;
Co. as nominee for The Depository Trust Company
(&lsquo;&lsquo;DTC&rsquo;&rsquo;). The records of DTC indicate that
as of March  31,  2006, there were: (i) twenty-seven (27)
DTC participants holding a position in the Class A-3 Notes 2.40%
and (ii) twenty-four (24) DTC participants holding a position in the
Class A-4 Notes 3.06%. The other previously issued classes are
no longer outstanding.</p>

99(A)</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top: 12pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff;">KPMG LLP</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff">Suite 2000<br>355 South
Grand Avenue<br>Los Angeles, CA 90071-1568</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: center; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top: 12pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff;">Independent
Accountants&rsquo; Report</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:17.04pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff">The Board of
Directors<br>American Honda Finance Corporation</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff">Members of
the Board:</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff">We have examined management&rsquo;s assertion
about American Honda Finance Corporation&rsquo;s (the Company)
compliance with the minimum servicing standards set forth in the
Mortgage Bankers Association of America <font style="font-weight: normal; font-style: italic">Uniform Single Attestation
Program for Mortgage Bankers</font>, as they relate to the servicing of
retail automobile loan contracts, as of and for the year ended
March  31,  2006 included in the accompanying
management&rsquo;s assertion. The minimum servicing standards not
considered by the Company to be applicable to the servicing of retail
automobile loans include procedures 2, 3, and 4 of Section I
&ndash; Custodial Bank Accounts, procedures 1, 2, 3, and 4
of Section III &ndash; Disbursements, and procedures 2, 3, and 4 of
Section V &ndash; Mortgage Loan Accounting. Management is responsible
for the Company&rsquo;s compliance with the applicable minimum
servicing standards. Our responsibility is to express an opinion on
management&rsquo;s assertion about the Company&rsquo;s compliance
based on our examination.</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff">Our examination was made in
accordance with standards established by the American Institute of
Certified Public Accountants and, accordingly, including examining, on
a test basis, evidence about the Company&rsquo;s compliance with the
minimum servicing standards and performing such other procedures as we
considered necessary in the circumstances. We believe that our
examination provides a reasonable basis for our opinion. Our
examination does not provide a legal determination on the
Company&rsquo;s compliance with the minimum servicing
standards.</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff">In our opinion, American Honda Finance
Corporation has complied, in all material respects, with the
aforementioned minimum servicing standards as of and for the year ended
March  31,  2006.</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff">This report is intended
solely for the information and use of management and the board of
directors, the Trustee, and the related beneficiaries and holders (as
defined in the Agreement of Definitions Relating to the Trust and
Servicing Agreement dated April  1,
1998).</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:24pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 0pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff">/s/ KPMG LLP</p>
<p style="font-family:serif;font-weight:normal;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;  width: 456pt; text-align: left; font-style: normal; line-height: 12pt; padding-top:6pt; padding-left:0pt; padding-right:0pt; padding-bottom: 6pt; margin: 0pt; text-indent: 0pt; background-color: #ffffff">June
